	1,
	'select one step related by self->SSTEP[R202];
LOG::LogSuccess( message:"finished " + step.name );
unrelate self from step across R202;
self.finish_step();

select one nextstep related by step->SSTEP[R107.''follows''];
if (empty nextstep)
	generate WRKEX3:''done'' to self;
else
	select one nexttask related by nextstep->WSTEP[R102];
	if (empty nexttask)	// this must be a repeat count specification
		LOG::LogInfo( message:nextstep.name );
		select one repeat related by nextstep->RSTEP[R102];		// it better be there...
		select many rspecs related by self->RSTEP[R203];	// are we already doing a repeat?
		repeating = FALSE;
		for each rep in rspecs
			if (rep == repeat)
				repeating = TRUE;
				break;	// we are already doing this set of reps..
			end if;
		end for;
		if (repeating == TRUE)
			select one counting related by repeat->RCOUNT[R203];
			if (counting.repeatCount == repeat.repeatCount)	// finished this repeat count
				unrelate repeat from self across R203 using counting;
				delete object instance counting;
			else
				counting.repeatCount = counting.repeatCount + 1; // not done yet; repeat once more
				select one nexttask related by repeat->WSTEP[R108];
				select one nextstep related by nexttask->SSTEP[R102];	// back again to start of repeat sequence
			end if;
		else
			create object instance counting of RCOUNT;	// set up a new repeat counter
			relate repeat to self across R203 using counting;
			counting.repeatCount = 1;	// start a set of repetitions
			select one nexttask related by repeat->WSTEP[R108];
			select one nextstep related by nexttask->SSTEP[R102];	// select start of this repeat sequence
		end if;
	end if;
	relate nextstep to self across R202;
	if (not_empty nexttask)	// we have an exercise step to perform
		self.init_step();
	else
		generate WRKEX2:''next'' to self;	// need to skip past this repeat spec.
	end if;
end if;
',
	'');
